<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pan, zoom, rotate, and flip with pointer, wheel, and pinch gestures</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Rectangle or circle crops with optional fixed area and aspect ratio</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Min/max crop dimensions and keyboard nudging</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Controlled zoom/rotation/flip with change callbacks</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Programmatic helpers like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.resize</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getCroppedImage</code></li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Accessibility labels, translations, and styling data attributes</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the image cropper correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="">No anatomy available for <!-- -->image-cropper</div>
<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the image cropper package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> imageCropper</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/image-cropper&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

</span><span class="code-line">          <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>span</span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-crop" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial crop<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-crop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Pass an <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialCrop</code> to start from a specific rectangle. The size is
constrained to your min/max and viewport, and the position is clamped within the
viewport.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">initialCrop</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">width</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">240</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">height</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">240</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">aspectRatio</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// optional, lock to square</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="fixed-crop-area" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Fixed crop area<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#fixed-crop-area"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Lock the crop window and allow only panning/zooming of the image beneath it by
setting <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">fixedCropArea: true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">fixedCropArea</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="crop-shape-and-aspect-ratio" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Crop shape and aspect ratio<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#crop-shape-and-aspect-ratio"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">cropShape</code> can be <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;rectangle&quot;</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;circle&quot;</code>.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aspectRatio</code> can lock the crop to a width/height ratio. When <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aspectRatio</code> is
not set and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">cropShape</code> is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;rectangle&quot;</code>, holding Shift while resizing locks
to the current ratio.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">cropShape</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;circle&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">aspectRatio</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// ignored for circle</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlling-zoom-rotation-and-flip" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling zoom, rotation, and flip<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-zoom-rotation-and-flip"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can configure defaults and limits, and also control them programmatically
using the API.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultZoom</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1.25</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">minZoom</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">maxZoom</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultRotation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultFlip</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">horizontal</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">vertical</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Programmatic controls</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setZoom</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// zoom to 2x</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setRotation</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">90</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// rotate to 90 degrees</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">flipHorizontally</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// toggle horizontal flip</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setFlip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">vertical</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// set vertical flip on</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-transform-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled transform values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-transform-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use controlled props and callbacks when transform values are managed by your
state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  zoom<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  rotation<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  flip<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onZoomChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setZoom</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">zoom</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onRotationChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setRotation</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">rotation</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFlipChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setFlip</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">flip</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-crop-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for crop changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-crop-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCropChange</code> to react when the crop rectangle changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onCropChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { crop: Rect }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">crop</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-resizing" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic resizing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-resizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.resize(handle, delta)</code> to resize from any handle programmatically.
Positive <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">delta</code> grows outward, negative shrinks inward.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Grow the selection by 8px from the right edge</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">resize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;right&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Shrink from top-left corner by 4px in both axes</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">resize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;top-left&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="getting-the-cropped-image" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Getting the cropped image<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#getting-the-cropped-image"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getCroppedImage</code> to export the current crop, taking
zoom/rotation/flip/pan into account.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Blob (default)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> blob <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword control-flow">await</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getCroppedImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;image/png&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">quality</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0.92</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Data URL</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> dataUrl <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword control-flow">await</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getCroppedImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">output</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;dataUrl&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;image/jpeg&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">quality</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0.85</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Example usage</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>blob<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token constant">URL</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createObjectURL</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>blob<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  previewImg<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">src</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> url
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="understanding-coordinate-systems" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Understanding coordinate systems<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#understanding-coordinate-systems"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The image cropper uses two different coordinate systems:</p>
<h4 id="1-viewport-coordinates-apicrop" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">1. Viewport Coordinates (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.crop</code>)<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#1-viewport-coordinates-apicrop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>These are the coordinates you see in the UI, relative to the visible viewport:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">crop</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// { x: 50, y: 30, width: 200, height: 150 }</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Characteristics:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Relative to the viewport dimensions</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Changes as you zoom and pan</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Perfect for UI rendering and controls</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Used by <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialCrop</code></li>
</ul>
<h4 id="2-natural-image-coordinates-apigetcropdata" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">2. Natural Image Coordinates (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getCropData()</code>)<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#2-natural-image-coordinates-apigetcropdata"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>These are the absolute pixel coordinates in the original image:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> cropData <span class="token operator">=</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getCropData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cropData<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// {</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   x: 250,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   y: 150,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   width: 1000,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   height: 750,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   rotate: 0,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   flipX: false,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//   flipY: false</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// }</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Characteristics:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Relative to the original image dimensions</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Independent of zoom/pan/viewport size</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Essential for server-side cropping</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Perfect for state persistence and undo/redo</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="when-to-use-each" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">When to use each<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#when-to-use-each"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p><strong>Use viewport coordinates (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.crop</code>)</strong> when:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Rendering UI controls (sliders, displays)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Setting initial crop area</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Building custom crop UI</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Use natural coordinates (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getCropData()</code>)</strong> when:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Sending crop data to your backend for server-side processing</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Persisting state (localStorage, database)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Implementing undo/redo functionality</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Exporting crop configuration to external tools</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="example-server-side-cropping" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Example: Server-side cropping<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#example-server-side-cropping"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Frontend: Get natural coordinates</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> cropData <span class="token operator">=</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getCropData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Send to backend</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword control-flow">await</span> <span class="token function">fetch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;/api/crop-image&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">method</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;POST&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">body</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token known-class-name class-name">JSON</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">stringify</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">imageId</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;photo-123&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">crop</span><span class="token operator">:</span> cropData<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// Natural pixel coordinates</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Backend: Crop the original image file</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Use cropData.x, cropData.y, cropData.width, cropData.height</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// to crop the actual image file at full resolution</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h4 id="transformation-example" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Transformation example<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#transformation-example"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>Here&#x27;s how the coordinates relate with a zoom of 2x:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Original image: 3000 × 2000 pixels</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Viewport: 600 × 400 pixels</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Zoom: 2x</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Viewport coordinates (what you see)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">crop</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// { x: 100, y: 80, width: 200, height: 150 }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Natural coordinates (original image)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getCropData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// { x: 500, y: 400, width: 1000, height: 750, ... }</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scale factor: 3000 / 600 = 5x</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// So 100px in viewport = 500px in original image</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="touch-and-wheel-gestures" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Touch and wheel gestures<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#touch-and-wheel-gestures"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use the mouse wheel over the viewport to zoom at the pointer location.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pinch with two fingers to zoom and pan; the machine smooths tiny changes and
tracks the pinch midpoint.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Drag on the viewport background to pan the image (when not dragging the
selection).</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="keyboard-nudges" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard nudges<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-nudges"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Configure keyboard nudge steps for move/resize:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">nudgeStep</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">nudgeStepShift</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">nudgeStepCtrl</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">The root is a live region with helpful descriptions of crop, zoom, and
rotation status.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">The selection exposes slider-like semantics to assistive tech and supports
keyboard movement, resizing (Alt+Arrows), and zooming (+/-).</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Customize accessible labels and descriptions via <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code>:</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageCropper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">rootLabel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Product image cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">selectionInstructions</span><span class="token operator">:</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">      <span class="token string">&quot;Use arrow keys to move, Alt+arrows to resize, and +/- to zoom.&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image-cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the root part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image-cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;viewport&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the viewport part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image-cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the image part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image-cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;selection&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the selection part */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;image-cropper&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;handle&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Moves the crop selection upward by the configured nudge step. Hold Shift for the `nudgeStepShift` value or Ctrl/Cmd for `nudgeStepCtrl`.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>Moves the crop selection downward by the configured nudge step. Hold Shift for the `nudgeStepShift` value or Ctrl/Cmd for `nudgeStepCtrl`.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div>Moves the crop selection to the left by the configured nudge step. Hold Shift for the `nudgeStepShift` value or Ctrl/Cmd for `nudgeStepCtrl`.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div>Moves the crop selection to the right by the configured nudge step. Hold Shift for the `nudgeStepShift` value or Ctrl/Cmd for `nudgeStepCtrl`.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Alt + ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Resizes the crop vertically from the bottom handle, reducing the height. Hold Shift or Ctrl/Cmd for the larger nudge steps.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Alt + ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>Resizes the crop vertically from the bottom handle, increasing the height. Hold Shift or Ctrl/Cmd for the larger nudge steps.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Alt + ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div>Resizes the crop horizontally from the right handle, reducing the width. Hold Shift or Ctrl/Cmd for the larger nudge steps.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Alt + ArrowRight</kbd></div><div>Resizes the crop horizontally from the right handle, increasing the width. Hold Shift or Ctrl/Cmd for the larger nudge steps.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">+</kbd></div><div>Zooms in on the image. The `=` key performs the same action on keyboards where both symbols share a key.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">-</kbd></div><div>Zooms out of the image. The `_` key performs the same action on keyboards where both symbols share a key.</div></li></ul>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The image cropper machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; viewport: string; image: string; selection: string; handle: (position: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the image cropper elements</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identify accessibility elements and their states.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">initialCrop</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Rect</code><span class="d_block">The initial rectangle of the crop area.
If not provided, a smart default will be computed based on viewport size and aspect ratio.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minWidth</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The minimum width of the crop area</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minHeight</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The minimum height of the crop area</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxWidth</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The maximum width of the crop area</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxHeight</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The maximum height of the crop area</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aspectRatio</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The aspect ratio to maintain for the crop area (width / height).
For example, an aspect ratio of 16 / 9 will maintain a width to height ratio of 16:9.
If not provided, the crop area can be freely resized.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">cropShape</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;rectangle&quot; | &quot;circle&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The shape of the crop area.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">zoom</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled zoom level of the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">rotation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The controlled rotation of the image in degrees (0 - 360).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">flip</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">FlipState</code><span class="d_block">The controlled flip state of the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultZoom</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial zoom factor to apply to the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultRotation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The initial rotation to apply to the image in degrees.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultFlip</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">FlipState</code><span class="d_block">The initial flip state to apply to the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">zoomStep</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The amount of zoom applied per wheel step.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">zoomSensitivity</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">Controls how responsive pinch-to-zoom is.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minZoom</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The minimum zoom factor allowed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxZoom</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The maximum zoom factor allowed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">nudgeStep</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The base nudge step for keyboard arrow keys (in pixels).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">nudgeStepShift</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The nudge step when Shift key is held (in pixels).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">nudgeStepCtrl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The nudge step when Ctrl/Cmd key is held (in pixels).</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onZoomChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ZoomChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback fired when the zoom level changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRotationChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: RotationChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback fired when the rotation changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFlipChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: FlipChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback fired when the flip state changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCropChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: CropChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback fired when the crop area changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">fixedCropArea</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the crop area is fixed in size and position.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The image cropper <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px of the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold prose">flip</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">FlipState</code><span class="d_block">The current flip state of the image.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">crop</code><code class="fs_sm Returns a Promise that resolves to either a Blob or data URL.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getCropData</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; CropData</code><span class="d_block">Function to get the crop data in natural image pixel coordinates.
These coordinates are relative to the original image dimensions,
accounting for zoom, rotation, and flip transformations.
Use this for server-side cropping or state persistence.</span></li></ul>

cropper lets users select and edit an image crop area with pan, zoom,\nrotation, and flip controls.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/image-cropper\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"ImageCropper\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePan, zoom, rotate, and flip with pointer, wheel, and pinch gestures\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRectangle or circle crops with optional fixed area and aspect ratio\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMin/max crop dimensions and keyboard nudging\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eControlled zoom/rotation/flip with change callbacks\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eProgrammatic helpers like \u003ccode\u003eapi.resize\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eapi.getCroppedImage\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAccessibility labels, translations, and styling data attributes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the image cropper package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"image-cropper/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo set up the image cropper correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"image-cropper\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the image cropper package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as imageCropper from \"@zag-js/image-cropper\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"image-cropper/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial crop\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass an \u003ccode\u003einitialCrop\u003c/code\u003e to start from a specific rectangle. The size is\nconstrained to your min/max and viewport, and the position is clamped within the\nviewport.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  initialCrop: { x: 40, y: 40, width: 240, height: 240 },\n  aspectRatio: 1, // optional, lock to square\n})\nconst api = imageCropper.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFixed crop area\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eLock the crop window and allow only panning/zooming of the image beneath it by\nsetting \u003ccode\u003efixedCropArea: true\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  fixedCropArea: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCrop shape and aspect ratio\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecropShape\u003c/code\u003e can be \u003ccode\u003e\"rectangle\"\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e\"circle\"\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003easpectRatio\u003c/code\u003e can lock the crop to a width/height ratio. When \u003ccode\u003easpectRatio\u003c/code\u003e is\nnot set and \u003ccode\u003ecropShape\u003c/code\u003e is \u003ccode\u003e\"rectangle\"\u003c/code\u003e, holding Shift while resizing locks\nto the current ratio.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  cropShape: \"circle\",\n  aspectRatio: 1, // ignored for circle\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling zoom, rotation, and flip\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can configure defaults and limits, and also control them programmatically\nusing the API.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  defaultZoom: 1.25,\n  minZoom: 1,\n  maxZoom: 5,\n  defaultRotation: 0,\n  defaultFlip: { horizontal: false, vertical: false },\n})\nconst api = imageCropper.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n// Programmatic controls\napi.setZoom(2) // zoom to 2x\napi.setRotation(90) // rotate to 90 degrees\napi.flipHorizontally() // toggle horizontal flip\napi.setFlip({ vertical: true }) // set vertical flip on\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled transform values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse controlled props and callbacks when transform values are managed by your\nstate.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  zoom,\n  rotation,\n  flip,\n  onZoomChange(details) {\n    setZoom(details.zoom)\n  },\n  onRotationChange(details) {\n    setRotation(details.rotation)\n  },\n  onFlipChange(details) {\n    setFlip(details.flip)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for crop changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonCropChange\u003c/code\u003e to react when the crop rectangle changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  onCropChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { crop: Rect }\n    console.log(details.crop)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eProgrammatic resizing\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eapi.resize(handle, delta)\u003c/code\u003e to resize from any handle programmatically.\nPositive \u003ccode\u003edelta\u003c/code\u003e grows outward, negative shrinks inward.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// Grow the selection by 8px from the right edge\napi.resize(\"right\", 8)\n// Shrink from top-left corner by 4px in both axes\napi.resize(\"top-left\", -4)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eGetting the cropped image\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eapi.getCroppedImage\u003c/code\u003e to export the current crop, taking\nzoom/rotation/flip/pan into account.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// Blob (default)\nconst blob = await api.getCroppedImage({ type: \"image/png\", quality: 0.92 })\n\n// Data URL\nconst dataUrl = await api.getCroppedImage({\n  output: \"dataUrl\",\n  type: \"image/jpeg\",\n  quality: 0.85,\n})\n\n// Example usage\nif (blob) {\n  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)\n  previewImg.src = url\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUnderstanding coordinate systems\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe image cropper uses two different coordinate systems:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e1. Viewport Coordinates (\u003ccode\u003eapi.crop\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the coordinates you see in the UI, relative to the visible viewport:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econsole.log(api.crop)\n// { x: 50, y: 30, width: 200, height: 150 }\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCharacteristics:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRelative to the viewport dimensions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChanges as you zoom and pan\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePerfect for UI rendering and controls\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUsed by \u003ccode\u003einitialCrop\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003e2. Natural Image Coordinates (\u003ccode\u003eapi.getCropData()\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the absolute pixel coordinates in the original image:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst cropData = api.getCropData()\nconsole.log(cropData)\n// {\n//   x: 250,\n//   y: 150,\n//   width: 1000,\n//   height: 750,\n//   rotate: 0,\n//   flipX: false,\n//   flipY: false\n// }\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCharacteristics:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRelative to the original image dimensions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIndependent of zoom/pan/viewport size\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEssential for server-side cropping\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePerfect for state persistence and undo/redo\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eWhen to use each\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUse viewport coordinates (\u003ccode\u003eapi.crop\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/strong\u003e when:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRendering UI controls (sliders, displays)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSetting initial crop area\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBuilding custom crop UI\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUse natural coordinates (\u003ccode\u003eapi.getCropData()\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/strong\u003e when:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSending crop data to your backend for server-side processing\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePersisting state (localStorage, database)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eImplementing undo/redo functionality\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExporting crop configuration to external tools\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eExample: Server-side cropping\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// Frontend: Get natural coordinates\nconst cropData = api.getCropData()\n\n// Send to backend\nawait fetch(\"/api/crop-image\", {\n  method: \"POST\",\n  body: JSON.stringify({\n    imageId: \"photo-123\",\n    crop: cropData, // Natural pixel coordinates\n  }),\n})\n\n// Backend: Crop the original image file\n// Use cropData.x, cropData.y, cropData.width, cropData.height\n// to crop the actual image file at full resolution\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eTransformation example\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHere's how the coordinates relate with a zoom of 2x:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// Original image: 3000 × 2000 pixels\n// Viewport: 600 × 400 pixels\n// Zoom: 2x\n\n// Viewport coordinates (what you see)\napi.crop\n// { x: 100, y: 80, width: 200, height: 150 }\n\n// Natural coordinates (original image)\napi.getCropData()\n// { x: 500, y: 400, width: 1000, height: 750, ... }\n// Scale factor: 3000 / 600 = 5x\n// So 100px in viewport = 500px in original image\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eTouch and wheel gestures\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse the mouse wheel over the viewport to zoom at the pointer location.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePinch with two fingers to zoom and pan; the machine smooths tiny changes and\ntracks the pinch midpoint.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDrag on the viewport background to pan the image (when not dragging the\nselection).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eKeyboard nudges\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eConfigure keyboard nudge steps for move/resize:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  nudgeStep: 1,\n  nudgeStepShift: 10,\n  nudgeStepCtrl: 50,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAccessibility\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe root is a live region with helpful descriptions of crop, zoom, and\nrotation status.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe selection exposes slider-like semantics to assistive tech and supports\nkeyboard movement, resizing (Alt+Arrows), and zooming (+/-).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCustomize accessible labels and descriptions via \u003ccode\u003etranslations\u003c/code\u003e:\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(imageCropper.machine, {\n  translations: {\n    rootLabel: \"Product image cropper\",\n    selectionInstructions:\n      \"Use arrow keys to move, Alt+arrows to resize, and +/- to zoom.\",\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute you can target in CSS.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-scope=\"image-cropper\"][data-part=\"root\"] {\n  /* styles for the root part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"image-cropper\"][data-part=\"viewport\"] {\n  /* styles for the viewport part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"image-cropper\"][data-part=\"image\"] {\n  /* styles for the image part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"image-cropper\"][data-part=\"selection\"] {\n  /* styles for the selection part */\n}\n\n[data-scope=\"image-cropper\"][data-part=\"handle\"] {\n  /* styles for the handle part */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelection shapes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe selection can be styled based on its shape:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"selection\"][data-shape=\"circle\"] {\n  /* styles for circular selection */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"selection\"][data-shape=\"rectangle\"] {\n  /* styles for rectangular selection */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eStates\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eVarious states can be styled using data attributes:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"][data-dragging] {\n  /* styles when dragging the selection */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-fixed] {\n  /* styles when the crop area is fixed */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eKeyboard Interactions\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003ckeyboardtable name=\"image-cropper\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eMethods and
